D
FORTRAN Subroutines
Multiple FORTRAN subroutines of the existing pmlib software have been modiﬁed in
this project. Further, some additional subroutines are programmed. Some subroutines,
which have been a main part of this project, are shown below in this chapter as:
• flowcases_bump_ring.f
The bump vortex ring setup with the correction of the circulation for normalization.
• flowcases_bump_roller.f
The bump vortex roller setup with an added wave perturbation along the centerline.
• flowcases_gaussian_roller.f
The Gaussian vortex roller setup with an added wave perturbation along the cen-
terline.
• part_deriv_vorticity.f
The added O(h6) and O(h8) Finite Diﬀerence schemes for the calculation of the
particle derivatives in the discretized vorticity equation
143
==PAGE:160==
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! flowcases_bump_ring.f
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! <<HEADER>>
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Initializes vorticity field as a "bump" vortex ring
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
SUBROUTINE flowcases_bump_ring(topo,mesh,ierr)
USE pmlib_mod_topology
USE pmlib_mod_mesh
IMPLICIT NONE
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Arguments
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  TYPE(class_topology),DIMENSION(:),POINTER    :: topo
  TYPE(class_mesh)                             :: mesh
  INTEGER, INTENT(OUT)                         :: ierr
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Local variables
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  CHARACTER(LEN=18)                            :: caller='flowcase_bump_ring'
  REAL(MK)                                     :: PI
  INTEGER                                      :: i,j,k
  REAL(MK)                                     :: px,py,pz
  REAL(MK),DIMENSION(ndim)                     :: xmin, dx
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(ndim)                      :: ncell
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(2*ndim)                    :: nghost
  REAL(MK)                                     :: max_vort
  REAL(MK)                                     :: r,r0
  REAL(MK)                                     :: rho, phi, theta
  REAL(MK)                                     :: sigma0, sigma
  REAL(MK)                                     :: vort_mag
  REAL(MK)                                     :: Gamma_Cor 
  REAL(MK)                                     :: circulation_pos, circulation_neg
  REAL(MK)                                     :: sum_circ1, sum_circ2
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Initiate subroutine
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ierr = 0
  PI = ACOS(-1.0_MK)
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Setup initial vorticity field for calculation Gamma correction
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  r0       = 0.5_MK
==PAGE:161==
  vort_max = 1.0_MK
  sum_circ1 = 0.0_MK
  sum_circ2 = 0.0_MK
  dx     = topo(rank)%dx
  xmin   = topo(rank)%xmin
  ncell  = topo(rank)%ncell
  nghost = topo(rank)%nghost
  mesh%vort = 0.0_MK
  mesh%vel = 0.0_MK
  
  DO k = 1-nghost(5),ncell(3)+nghost(6)
     pz = xmin(3) + (REAL(k - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(3)
     DO j = 1-nghost(3),ncell(2)+nghost(4)
        py = xmin(2) + (REAL(j - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(2)
        DO i = 1-nghost(1),ncell(1)+nghost(2)
           px = xmin(1) + (REAL(i - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(1)
           rho   = SQRT(pz*pz + py*py)
           phi   = SQRT((rho - r0)**2 + px**2)
           theta = ATAN2(pz,py)
           IF ( phi .LT. r0) THEN
              vort_mag = ( -EXP(- c_bump*r0**2/(2.0_MK*r0*rho - rho**2 - px**2)) * &
                   & ( 4.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**4*px**2*rho**2 &
                   & - 16.0_MK*r0**4*rho**4 &
                   & + 32.0_MK*r0**3*rho**5 &
                   & - 24.0_MK*r0**2*rho**6 &
                   & + 8.0_MK*r0*rho**7 & 
                   & - 4.0_MK*rho**6*px**2 &
                   & - 6.0_MK*rho**4*px**4 & 
                   & - 4.0_MK*rho**2*px**6 &
                   & - 8.0_MK*c_bump*r0**5*rho**3 &
                   & + 8.0_MK*c_bump*r0**4*rho**4 &
                   & - 6.0_MK*c_bump*r0**3*rho**5 & 
                   & + 4.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**6*rho**2 &
                   & - 8.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**5*rho**3 & 
                   & + 4.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**4*rho**4 & 
                   & + 2.0_MK*c_bump*r0**2*rho**6 &
                   & + 32.0_MK*r0**3*rho**3*px**2 &
                   & - 48.0_MK*r0**2*rho**4*px**2 &
                   & - 24.0_MK*r0**2*rho**2*px**4 & 
                   & + 24.0_MK*r0*rho**5*px**2 &
                   & + 24.0_MK*r0*rho**3*px**4 & 
                   & + 8.0_MK*r0*rho*px**6 & 
                   & + 2.0_MK*c_bump*r0**3*rho*px**4 &
                   & + 2.0_MK*c_bump*r0**2*rho**2*px**4 &
==PAGE:162==
                   & - 4.0_MK*c_bump*r0**3*rho**3*px**2 & 
                   & + 4.0_MK*c_bump*r0**2*rho**4*px**2 & 
                   & - rho**8 - px**8) & 
                   & * (2.0_MK*r0*rho - rho**2 - px**2)**(-4)*rho**(-2) &
                   & / ( EXP(-c_bump)*(4.0_MK*c_bump + 1.0_MK)/r0**2 ))
              mesh%vort(1,i,j,k) =   0.0_MK 
              mesh%vort(2,i,j,k) = - SIN(theta)*vort_mag
              mesh%vort(3,i,j,k) =   COS(theta)*vort_mag
              ! Calculate initial circulation
              
              IF (mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3) .GT. 0.0_MK) THEN
                sum_circ1 = sum_circ1 + SIGN(1.0_MK, py)*mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3)
              ELSEIF (mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3) .LT. 0.0_MK) THEN
                sum_circ2 = sum_circ2 + SIGN(1.0_MK, py)*mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3)
              ENDIF
           ELSE
              mesh%vort(1,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
              mesh%vort(2,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
              mesh%vort(3,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
           ENDIF
        END DO !i
     END DO !j
  END DO !k
  PRINT *, 'sum_circ1 b_Corr:', sum_circ1
  PRINT *, 'sum_circ2 b_Corr:' ,sum_circ2 
  
  CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE(sum_circ1, circulation_pos, 1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_SUM,0,comm,ierr)
  CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE(sum_circ2, circulation_neg, 1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_SUM,0,comm,ierr)
  PRINT *, 'circulation_pos b_Corr', circulation_pos
  PRINT *, 'circulation_neg b_Corr', circulation_neg
   
  Gamma_Cor = (circulation_pos+circulation_neg)/2.0_MK
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Setup initial vorticity field normalized with Gamma_Cor
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  r0       = 0.5_MK
  vort_max = 1.0_MK
  sum_circ1 = 0.0_MK
  sum_circ2 = 0.0_MK
  dx     = topo(rank)%dx
  xmin   = topo(rank)%xmin
==PAGE:163==
  ncell  = topo(rank)%ncell
  nghost = topo(rank)%nghost
  mesh%vort = 0.0_MK
  mesh%vel = 0.0_MK
  
  DO k = 1-nghost(5),ncell(3)+nghost(6)
     pz = xmin(3) + (REAL(k - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(3)
     DO j = 1-nghost(3),ncell(2)+nghost(4)
        py = xmin(2) + (REAL(j - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(2)
        DO i = 1-nghost(1),ncell(1)+nghost(2)
           px = xmin(1) + (REAL(i - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(1)
           rho   = SQRT(pz*pz + py*py)
           phi   = SQRT((rho - r0)**2 + px**2)
           theta = ATAN2(pz,py)
           IF ( phi .LT. r0) THEN
              vort_mag = 1.0_MK/Gamma_Cor*( -EXP(- c_bump*r0**2/(2.0_MK*r0*rho - rho**2 - 
px**2)) * &
                   & ( 4.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**4*px**2*rho**2 &
                   & - 16.0_MK*r0**4*rho**4 &
                   & + 32.0_MK*r0**3*rho**5 &
                   & - 24.0_MK*r0**2*rho**6 &
                   & + 8.0_MK*r0*rho**7 & 
                   & - 4.0_MK*rho**6*px**2 &
                   & - 6.0_MK*rho**4*px**4 & 
                   & - 4.0_MK*rho**2*px**6 &
                   & - 8.0_MK*c_bump*r0**5*rho**3 &
                   & + 8.0_MK*c_bump*r0**4*rho**4 &
                   & - 6.0_MK*c_bump*r0**3*rho**5 & 
                   & + 4.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**6*rho**2 &
                   & - 8.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**5*rho**3 & 
                   & + 4.0_MK*c_bump**2*r0**4*rho**4 & 
                   & + 2.0_MK*c_bump*r0**2*rho**6 &
                   & + 32.0_MK*r0**3*rho**3*px**2 &
                   & - 48.0_MK*r0**2*rho**4*px**2 &
                   & - 24.0_MK*r0**2*rho**2*px**4 & 
                   & + 24.0_MK*r0*rho**5*px**2 &
                   & + 24.0_MK*r0*rho**3*px**4 & 
                   & + 8.0_MK*r0*rho*px**6 & 
                   & + 2.0_MK*c_bump*r0**3*rho*px**4 &
                   & + 2.0_MK*c_bump*r0**2*rho**2*px**4 &
                   & - 4.0_MK*c_bump*r0**3*rho**3*px**2 & 
                   & + 4.0_MK*c_bump*r0**2*rho**4*px**2 & 
                   & - rho**8 - px**8) & 
                   & * (2.0_MK*r0*rho - rho**2 - px**2)**(-4)*rho**(-2) &
                   & / ( EXP(-c_bump)*(4.0_MK*c_bump + 1.0_MK)/r0**2 ))
==PAGE:164==
              mesh%vort(1,i,j,k) =   0.0_MK 
              mesh%vort(2,i,j,k) = - SIN(theta)*vort_mag
              mesh%vort(3,i,j,k) =   COS(theta)*vort_mag
              ! Calculate initial circulation
              
              IF (mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3) .GT. 0.0_MK) THEN
                sum_circ1 = sum_circ1 + SIGN(1.0_MK, py)*mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3)
              ELSEIF (mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3) .LT. 0.0_MK) THEN
                sum_circ2 = sum_circ2 + SIGN(1.0_MK, py)*mesh%vort(3,i,j,k)*dx(1)*dx(3)
              ENDIF
           ELSE
              mesh%vort(1,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
              mesh%vort(2,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
              mesh%vort(3,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
           ENDIF
        END DO !i
     END DO !j
  END DO !k
  PRINT *, 'sum_circ1: a_Corr', sum_circ1
  PRINT *, 'sum_circ2: a_Corr' ,sum_circ2 
  
  CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE(sum_circ1, circulation_pos, 1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_SUM,0,comm,ierr)
  CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE(sum_circ2, circulation_neg, 1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_SUM,0,comm,ierr)
  PRINT *, 'circulation_pos a_Corr', circulation_pos
  PRINT *, 'circulation_neg a_Corr', circulation_neg  
  
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Return
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
 9999 CONTINUE
RETURN
END SUBROUTINE flowcases_bump_ring
==PAGE:165==
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! flowcases_bump_roller.f
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! <<HEADER>>
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
SUBROUTINE flowcases_bump_roller_pertubation(patch,topo,mesh,ierr)
  
  USE pmlib_mod_topology
  USE pmlib_mod_patch
  USE pmlib_mod_mesh
  IMPLICIT NONE
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Arguments
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  TYPE(class_patch)                            :: patch
!  TYPE(class_topology)                         :: topo
  TYPE(class_mesh)                             :: mesh
  INTEGER, INTENT(OUT)                         :: ierr
TYPE(class_topology),DIMENSION(:),POINTER    :: topo
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Local variables
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  CHARACTER(LEN=20)                            :: caller='flowcases_bump_roller_pertubation'
  REAL(MK)                                     :: t0
  
  INTEGER                                      :: i,j,k,n
  REAL(MK)                                     :: px,py,pz
  REAL(MK)                                     :: PI
  REAL(MK),DIMENSION(ndim)                     :: xmin, dx
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(ndim)                      :: ncell
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(2*ndim)                    :: nghost
  REAL(MK)                                     :: vort_z, max_vort, sum_vort_z, max_vel
  REAL(MK)                                     :: rho,r0
  REAL(MK)                                     :: pertube_amplitude = 1.0E-7_MK
  INTEGER,PARAMETER                            :: pertube_num_modes = 64
  REAL(MK), DIMENSION(pertube_num_modes)       :: pertube_phases
  REAL(MK)                                     :: pertubation
  REAL(MK)                                     :: randmin, randmax, Lz
  
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Initiate subroutine
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  CALL substart(caller,t0,ierr)
!!! Determine length of domain in z-dir
  Lz    = patch%xmax(3)-patch%xmin(3)
==PAGE:166==
  PI = ACOS(-1.0_MK)
 PRINT *, 'Lz Initial:', Lz
 
!!! Generate random phases
  randmin = 0.0_MK
  randmax = 2.0_MK*PI
  CALL RANDOM_NUMBER(pertube_phases) 
  pertube_phases = randmin + (randmax-randmin)*pertube_phases
  
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Setup initial vorticity field
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  r0     = 0.5_MK
  dx     = topo(rank)%dx
  xmin   = topo(rank)%xmin
  ncell  = topo(rank)%ncell
  nghost = topo(rank)%nghost
  !dx     = topo%sub(rank)%dx
  !xmin   = topo%sub(rank)%xmin
  !ncell  = topo%sub(rank)%ncell
  !nghost = topo%sub(rank)%nghost
  mesh%vort = 0.0_MK
  mesh%vel = 0.0_MK
  max_vel = -0.2D1 / 0.3D1 / (-(-c_bump / 0.3D1 + 0.1D1 / 0.3D1 + sqrt(c_bump ** 2 &
       - 0.2D1 * c_bump + 0.4D1) / 0.3D1) / R0 ** 2 + 0.1D1) ** 2 * sqrt(0.3D1 &
       + 0.3D1 * sqrt(c_bump ** 2 - 0.2D1 * c_bump + 0.4D1) - 0.3D1 * c_bump) / R0 ** 2 &
       * c_bump * exp((0.1D1 - 0.1D1 / (-(-c_bump / 0.3D1 + 0.1D1 / 0.3D1 + sqrt(c_bump ** 2 &
       - 0.2D1 * c_bump + 0.4D1) / 0.3D1) / R0 ** 2 + 0.1D1)) * c_bump)
  sum_vort_z = 0.0_MK
  max_vort   = 0.0_MK
  DO k = 1-nghost(5),ncell(3)+nghost(6)
     pz = xmin(3) + (REAL(k - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(3)
     ! determine a pertubation
     pertubation = 0
     DO n = 1,pertube_num_modes
        pertubation = pertubation + SIN(n*2.0_MK*PI/Lz*pz+pertube_phases(n)) 
     END DO
     
     DO j = 1-nghost(3),ncell(2)+nghost(4)
        py = xmin(2) + (REAL(j - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(2)
        DO i = 1-nghost(1),ncell(1)+nghost(2)
           px = xmin(1) + (REAL(i - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(1)
           ! pertube centerline along x-axis
           px = px + pertube_amplitude*pertubation
           
           rho = SQRT(py*py + px*px) / R0
==PAGE:167==
           IF ( rho .LT. 1.0) THEN
             
              vort_z = 0.4D1 * (R0 ** 4 - (px ** 2 + py ** 2) * c_bump * R0 ** 2 &
                   & - (px ** 2 + py ** 2) ** 2) * R0 ** 2 &
                   & * exp(-(px ** 2 + py ** 2) * c_bump &
                   & / (R0 ** 2 - px ** 2 - py ** 2)) &
                   & * c_bump / (R0 ** 2 - px ** 2 - py ** 2) ** 4
              
           ELSE
              vort_z = 0.0_MK
           ENDIF
           ! scale
           vort_z = vort_z / abs(max_vel)
           
           mesh%vort(1,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
           mesh%vort(2,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
           mesh%vort(3,i,j,k) = vort_z
           ! find maximum vorticity
           max_vort = max( abs(vort_z) , max_vort)
           
        END DO !i
     END DO !j
  END DO !k
CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE( max_vort,vort_max,1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_MAX,comm,ierr  )
CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed in MPI_ALLREDUCE', *9999)
  write(*,*) max_vel, vort_max
! sum_vort_z = sum_vort_z / ncell(3)
! CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE( sum_vort_z,circ0,1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_SUM,comm,ierr  )
! CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed in MPI_ALLREDUCE', *9999)
! write(*,*) circ0
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Return
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
9999 CONTINUE
  CALL substop(caller,t0,ierr)
END SUBROUTINE flowcases_bump_roller_pertubation
==PAGE:168==
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! flowcases_bump_roller.f
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! <<HEADER>>
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
SUBROUTINE flowcases_gaussian_roller_pertubation(patch,topo,mesh,ierr)
  
  USE pmlib_mod_topology
  USE pmlib_mod_patch
  USE pmlib_mod_mesh
  IMPLICIT NONE
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Arguments
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  TYPE(class_topology),DIMENSION(:),POINTER    :: topo
  TYPE(class_mesh)                             :: mesh
  INTEGER, INTENT(OUT)                         :: ierr
  TYPE(class_patch)                            :: patch
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Local variables
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  CHARACTER(LEN=20)                            :: caller='flowcase_gaussian_roller'
  REAL(MK)                                     :: t0
  REAL(MK)                                     :: PI
  INTEGER                                      :: i,j,k,n
  REAL(MK)                                     :: px,py,pz
  REAL(MK),DIMENSION(ndim)                     :: xmin, dx
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(ndim)                      :: ncell
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(2*ndim)                    :: nghost
  REAL(MK)                                     :: vort_z, max_vort, sum_vort_z, max_vel
  REAL(MK)                                     :: rho,r0
  REAL(MK)                                     :: Gamma_Gaussian , sigma
  REAL(MK)                                     :: pertube_amplitude = 1.0E-7_MK
  INTEGER, PARAMETER                           :: pertube_num_modes = 24
  REAL(MK),DIMENSION(pertube_num_modes)        :: pertube_phases
  REAL(MK)                                     :: pertubation
  REAL(MK)                                     :: randmin, randmax, Lz
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Initiate subroutine
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  CALL substart(caller,t0,ierr)
   PI = ACOS(-1.0_MK)
   Lz = patch%xmax(3)-patch%xmin(3)
==PAGE:169==
   randmin = 0.0_MK
   randmax = 2.0_MK*PI
   CALL RANDOM_NUMBER(pertube_phases)
   pertube_phases = randmin + (randmax-randmin)*pertube_phases
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Setup initial vorticity field
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
 ! r0       = 0.5_MK
  Gamma_Gaussian = 1.0_MK
  !sigma    = ring_core_size
  sigma = 0.06_MK
  R0     = 2.1_MK*sigma  
  dx     = topo(rank)%dx
  xmin   = topo(rank)%xmin
  ncell  = topo(rank)%ncell
  nghost = topo(rank)%nghost
  mesh%vort = 0.0_MK
  mesh%vel = 0.0_MK
  sum_vort_z = 0.0_MK
  max_vort   = 0.0_MK
  DO k = 1-nghost(5),ncell(3)+nghost(6)
     pz = xmin(3) + (REAL(k - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(3)
     pertubation = 0
     DO n = 1,pertube_num_modes
        pertubation = pertubation + SIN(n*2.0_MK*PI/Lz*pz+pertube_phases(n))
     END DO
     DO j = 1-nghost(3),ncell(2)+nghost(4)
        py = xmin(2) + (REAL(j - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(2)
        DO i = 1-nghost(1),ncell(1)+nghost(2)
           px = xmin(1) + (REAL(i - 1,MK) + 0.5_MK) *dx(1)
           
           px = px + pertube_amplitude*pertubation
           rho = SQRT(py*py + px*px) / R0
           IF ( rho .LT. 1.0) THEN
             
              vort_z = Gamma_Gaussian / (PI*sigma**2)*EXP(-(px**2+py**2)/sigma**2)
           ELSE
              vort_z = 0.0_MK
==PAGE:170==
           ENDIF
          
           mesh%vort(1,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
           mesh%vort(2,i,j,k) = 0.0_MK
           mesh%vort(3,i,j,k) = vort_z
           ! find maximum vorticity
           max_vort = max( abs(vort_z) , max_vort)
           
        END DO !i
     END DO !j
  END DO !k
CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE( max_vort,vort_max,1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_MAX,comm,ierr  )
CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed in MPI_ALLREDUCE', *9999)
  write(*,*) max_vel, vort_max
! sum_vort_z = sum_vort_z / ncell(3)
! CALL MPI_ALLREDUCE( sum_vort_z,circ0,1,mpi_prec_real,MPI_SUM,comm,ierr  )
! CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed in MPI_ALLREDUCE', *9999)
! write(*,*) circ0
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! Return
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
9999 CONTINUE
  CALL substop(caller,t0,ierr)
END SUBROUTINE flowcases_gaussian_roller_pertubation
==PAGE:171==
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! part_deriv_vorticity.f
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
! This routines computes and increments the vorticity equation
! Dω/Dt = (ω
)u + ν ²ω (stretching + molecular diffusion )
⋅∇
∇
! NOTE: ghosts of field (DωDt) IS mapped
!---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
SUBROUTINE part_deriv_vorticity(patch,topo_all,mesh,ierr,clear)
  USE pmlib_mod_topology
  USE pmlib_mod_mesh
  USE pmlib_mod_communication
  USE mod_penalisation    ! for clearence within solid
  IMPLICIT NONE
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ! Arguments
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  TYPE(class_patch),DIMENSION(:,:),POINTER,INTENT(IN)         :: patch
  TYPE(class_topology_all),DIMENSION(:,:),POINTER,INTENT(IN)  :: topo_all
  TYPE(class_mesh),DIMENSION(:,:),POINTER,INTENT(INOUT)       :: mesh
  INTEGER, INTENT(OUT)                                        :: ierr
  LOGICAL, INTENT(IN), OPTIONAL                               :: clear
  
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ! Local variables
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  CHARACTER(LEN=20)
                       :: caller='part_deriv_vorticity'
  INTEGER                                      :: i,j,k,l
  INTEGER                                      :: ilevel,ipatch
  REAL(MK),DIMENSION(ndim)                     :: dx
  INTEGER,DIMENSION(ndim)                      :: ncell
  REAL(MK)                                     :: w1, w2, w3
  REAL(MK)                                     :: ddwdx, ddwdy, ddwdz
  REAL(MK),DIMENSION(ndim,ndim)                :: dudx
  REAL(MK)                                     :: c_1_dx2, c_1_2dx
  REAL(MK)                                     :: c_1_dy2, c_1_2dy
  REAL(MK)                                     :: c_1_dz2, c_1_2dz
  REAL(MK)                                     :: c1, c2, c3, c4, c5
  REAL(MK)                                     :: c6, c7, c8, c9
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ! Initiate subroutine
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ierr = 0
==PAGE:172==
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  ! Clear mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort - default is TRUE
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------
  IF( ( PRESENT(clear) .AND. clear ) .OR. ( .NOT. PRESENT(clear)) ) THEN
     DO ilevel = 1,pmlib_nlevel
        DO ipatch = 1,pmlib_npatch(ilevel)
           mesh(ilevel, ipatch)%dvort = 0.0_MK
        END DO
     END DO
  END IF
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ! Calculate right-hand-side of the vorticity equation
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  DO ilevel = 1,pmlib_nlevel
     DO ipatch = 1,pmlib_npatch(ilevel)
        ncell  = topo_all(ilevel,ipatch)%cuboid(rank)%ncell
        dx     = topo_all(ilevel,ipatch)%cuboid(rank)%dx
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     ! 6th order FD
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ELSE IF (pmlib_fd_order .EQ. 6) THEN
  
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     ! Setup irrationel coefficients for the finite difference stencils
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     c_1_dx2 = 1.0_MK/(dx(1)**2)
     c_1_dy2 = 1.0_MK/(dx(2)**2)
     c_1_dz2 = 1.0_MK/(dx(3)**2)
  
     c_1_2dx = 1.0_MK/(2.0_MK*dx(1))
     c_1_2dy = 1.0_MK/(2.0_MK*dx(2))
     c_1_2dz = 1.0_MK/(2.0_MK*dx(3))
  
 ! second derivative coeff.
     c1 =     2.0_MK/180.0_MK
     c2 = -  27.0_MK/180.0_MK
 c3 =   270.0_MK/180.0_MK
     c4 = - 490.0_MK/180.0_MK
 
 ! first derivative coeff.
     c5 = -   1.0_MK/30.0_MK
     c6 =     9.0_MK/30.0_MK
     c7 = -  45.0_MK/30.0_MK
 
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     ! Calculate the particle derivative
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     DO k = 1,ncell(3)
        DO j = 1,ncell(2)
           DO i = 1,ncell(1)
==PAGE:173==
  
             !w1 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(1,i,j,k)
             !w2 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(2,i,j,k)
             !w3 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(3,i,j,k)
              ! use large scale vorticity (calculated in poisson solver) for stretching
              w1 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(1,i,j,k)
              w2 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(2,i,j,k)
              w3 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(3,i,j,k)
 ! PRINT *, 'k - n+3',i,j,k,mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(1,i,j,ncell(3)+3),ncell(3)  
 ! PRINT *, 'k - n+3',i,j,k,mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel (1,i,j,ncell(3)+3),ncell(3)  
              DO l = 1,pmlib_ndim
                 ! x-derivative
                 ddwdx     = (c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-3,j,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-2,j,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-1,j,k) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i  ,j,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+1,j,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+2,j,k) &
                      & +     c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+3,j,k) &  
                      & ) * c_1_dx2
                 dudx(l,1) = (c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-3,j,k) &
                      & +     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-2,j,k) & 
                      & +     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-1,j,k) & 
                      & -     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+1,j,k) & 
                      & -     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+2,j,k) & 
                      & -     c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+3,j,k) & 
                      & ) * c_1_2dx
                 ! y-derivative
                 ddwdy     = (c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-3,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-2,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-1,k) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j  ,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+1,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+2,k) &
                      & +     c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+3,k) &  
                      & ) * c_1_dy2
                 dudx(l,2) = (c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-3,k) &
                      & +     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-2,k) & 
                      & +     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-1,k) & 
                      & -     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+1,k) & 
                      & -     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+2,k) & 
                      & -     c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+3,k) & 
                      & ) * c_1_2dy
                 ! z-derivative
                 ddwdz     = (c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-3) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-2) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-1) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k  ) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+1) &
==PAGE:174==
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+2) &
                      & +     c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+3) &
                      & ) * c_1_dz2
                 dudx(l,3) = (c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-3) &
                      & +     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-2) & 
                      & +     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-1) & 
                      & -     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+1) & 
                      & -     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+2) & 
                      & -     c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+3) & 
                      & ) * c_1_2dz
  
                 ! The 3D vorticity equation
                 mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort(l,i,j,k) = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort(l,i,j,k) &
                      & + visc * (ddwdx + ddwdy + ddwdz) &
                      & + w1*dudx(l,1) + w2*dudx(l,2) + w3*dudx(l,3)
              END DO
  
           END DO
        END DO
     END DO
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     ! 8th order FD
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ELSE IF (pmlib_fd_order .EQ. 8) THEN
  
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     ! Setup irrationel coefficients for the finite difference stencils
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     c_1_dx2 = 1.0_MK/(dx(1)**2)
     c_1_dy2 = 1.0_MK/(dx(2)**2)
     c_1_dz2 = 1.0_MK/(dx(3)**2)
  
     c_1_2dx = 1.0_MK/(2.0_MK*dx(1))
     c_1_2dy = 1.0_MK/(2.0_MK*dx(2))
     c_1_2dz = 1.0_MK/(2.0_MK*dx(3))
  
     ! second derivative coeff.
     c1 = -     9.0_MK/5040.0_MK
     c2 =     128.0_MK/5040.0_MK
 c3 = -  1008.0_MK/5040.0_MK
     c4 =    8064.0_MK/5040.0_MK
 c5 = - 14350.0_MK/5040.0_MK
 
 ! first derivative coeff.
     c6 =     3.0_MK/420.0_MK
     c7 = -  32.0_MK/420.0_MK
 c8 =   168.0_MK/420.0_MK
 c9 = - 672.0_MK/420.0_MK
 
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     ! Calculate the particle derivative
==PAGE:175==
     !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
     DO k = 1,ncell(3)
        DO j = 1,ncell(2)
           DO i = 1,ncell(1)
  
             !w1 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(1,i,j,k)
             !w2 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(2,i,j,k)
             !w3 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(3,i,j,k)
              ! use large scale vorticity (calculated in poisson solver) for stretching
              w1 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(1,i,j,k)
              w2 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(2,i,j,k)
              w3 = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(3,i,j,k)
  
              DO l = 1,pmlib_ndim
                 ! x-derivative
                 ddwdx     = (c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-4,j,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-3,j,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-2,j,k) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i-1,j,k) &
                      & +     c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i  ,j,k) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+1,j,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+2,j,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+3,j,k) &  
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i+4,j,k) &  
                      & ) * c_1_dx2
                 dudx(l,1) = (c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-4,j,k) &
                      & +     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-3,j,k) & 
                      & +     c8 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-2,j,k) & 
                      & +     c9 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i-1,j,k) & 
                      & -     c9 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+1,j,k) & 
                      & -     c8 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+2,j,k) & 
                      & -     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+3,j,k) & 
                      & -     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i+4,j,k) & 
                      & ) * c_1_2dx
                 ! y-derivative
                 ddwdy     = (c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-4,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-3,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-2,k) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j-1,k) &
                      & +     c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j  ,k) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+1,k) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+2,k) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+3,k) &
                      & +     c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j+4,k) &  
                      & ) * c_1_dy2
                 dudx(l,2) = (c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-4,k) &
                      & +     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-3,k) & 
                      & +     c8 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-2,k) & 
                      & +     c9 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j-1,k) & 
                      & -     c9 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+1,k) & 
                      & -     c8 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+2,k) & 
==PAGE:176==
                      & -     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+3,k) & 
                      & -     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j+4,k) & 
                      & ) * c_1_2dy
                 ! z-derivative
                 ddwdz     = (c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-4) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-3) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-2) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k-1) &
                      & +     c5 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k  ) &
                      & +     c4 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+1) &
                      & +     c3 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+2) &
                      & +     c2 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+3) &
                      & +     c1 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vort(l,i,j,k+4) &
                      & ) * c_1_dz2
                 dudx(l,3) = (c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-4) &
                      & +     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-3) & 
                      & +     c8 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-2) & 
                      & +     c9 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k-1) & 
                      & -     c9 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+1) & 
                      & -     c8 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+2) & 
                      & -     c7 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+3) & 
                      & -     c6 * mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%vel(l,i,j,k+4) & 
                      & ) * c_1_2dz
  
                 ! The 3D vorticity equation
                 mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort(l,i,j,k) = mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort(l,i,j,k) &
                      & + visc * (ddwdx + ddwdy + ddwdz) &
                      & + w1*dudx(l,1) + w2*dudx(l,2) + w3*dudx(l,3)
              END DO
  
           END DO
        END DO
     END DO
 
  ENDIF
  
        !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
        ! Map ghost cells
        !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
        DO i = 1,ndim
           CALL pmlib_mesh_map_ghost(topo_all(ilevel,ipatch)%cuboid, &
                & i,nvort,ierr,incl_edges = .FALSE.)
           CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed to map ghosts.', *9999)
           CALL pmlib_comm_pack(mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort,ierr)
           CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed to pack ghosts.', *9999)
           CALL pmlib_comm_send(ierr)
           CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed to send ghosts.', *9999)
           CALL pmlib_comm_unpack(topo_all(ilevel,ipatch)%cuboid, &
                & mesh(ilevel,ipatch)%dvort,0,ierr,clear=.FALSE.)
           CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed to unpack ghosts.', *9999)
           CALL pmlib_comm_finalise(ierr)
==PAGE:177==
           CALL chkierr(ierr,rank,caller,'Failed to to finalize comm. of ghosts.', *9999)
        END DO
     END DO ! ilevel
  END DO ! i patch
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
  ! Return
  !---------------------------------------------------------------------------------!
9999 CONTINUE
  RETURN
END SUBROUTINE part_deriv_vorticity
